Mr. Moon Sun-myung's Words Compilation Committee

Foreword
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
The Path of a Filial Son
<Prayer> Father! Today is September 10, 1972, and it is the second Sabbath of this month. On this morning, may Your mercy, compassion, and love be with us.
We are always lacking, always insufficient, and always immature, and we kneel and bow down this morning, longing for Your high grace. Our hearts must be like the hearts of children. Before Your great, high, and wide love, we must feel the depletion of life and have a heart that desires the liberation of freedom. 
Please provide us with the milk of life and guide us along the path of Your mercy. How can anyone present themselves before You? However, knowing the path of restoration that You have worked so hard to find us, we are reminded that You are our Father who has worked hard to find and meet us, and thus we have bowed down before You despite our shortcomings.
Without Your love, protection, and mercy, we are nothing but a group that must suffocate, aren't we? Father! As You come to us, please look after each of our hearts with Your fiery eyes, so that a sincere heart that can unite with Your nature may rise up within us.
On September 10, 1972 (Sunday), at the former headquarters church (Cheongpa-dong 1-ga).
* This message was also published in the April 1973 issue of <Unification World>.
8   The Path of a Filial Son
May we become those who live by Heaven, and may we learn to walk every path according to Heaven, for we know that this is how we become Your sons and daughters. We long for the day when we can stand before You without shame as Your sons and daughters, and we want to give You glory with all our strength and fulfill our duty of loyalty and filial piety. You know that this desire is earnest within us.
We are a miserable group that cannot escape the situation of being surrounded by an evil world and evil environment, and as we go, we stumble and fall, and in our fallen state, we struggle before You to receive Your assistance to rise again, only to fall once more. Yet, we know too well that we cannot help but follow the path You have taken, and we have a mission and responsibility to push forward, even if we must struggle. The more time passes, the more we feel the shame of not being able to face You, our Father. This is not the first or second time we have felt the heart of disloyalty. Father, please do not forsake us.
Please come to us with a heart of compassion, embrace us in Your heart, and allow us to cross the paths and hills that You must also cross with ease. When we are in a place of bleeding and falling, how much pain must You feel, and how many wounds must You bear alone to lead us? We did not realize that You are such a Father.
When we are sad, we complain before Heaven, and when we feel lonely, we often feel that loneliness more than we feel with Heaven, blaming Heaven and acting as if Heaven does not exist. Yet, when we think of how Heaven always comes to us despite our losses, we realize that we are not unhappy. We have become those who are in the most blessed position, yet we do not recognize that it is a blessed position. Now, we earnestly wish to become heavenly warriors who can run vigorously along the path of liberation for humanity that You have left in this world, possessing Your great heart and understanding Your wide heart.
9 
Father, this morning, please remember Your children scattered throughout South Korea. Although their situations and environments may differ, we know that their hearts, which wish to live for You and because of You, remain unchanged. Moreover, at this time, You know the sincere hearts we offer, so please remember this tragic situation where the North and South are divided.
There are ties of brotherhood that must be met, as well as ties of father and son, and the ties of husband and wife that have been crossed, and we know that You understand the sorrow of the Korean people. We do not rely on anyone in this world, nor do we depend on any power of the world; we can only rely on You and seek protection from You, Father.
May no one else be the master of this nation, and may Heaven alone be the master of this nation. Father, who knows the condition of this nation that no one can manage, please guide this nation according to Your plan and providence. Please remember the poor thirty million people in South Korea, and the fifteen million people in North Korea, Father.
The historical moment when the paths of Cain and Abel began to diverge… Perhaps, thinking of the painful boundary of the 38th parallel in this nation, we must forgive all the historical conditions of sorrow that have arisen. As we consider this as the condition of Heaven until now, the more we think about it, the more we realize that we are in the heart of a Father whose feelings cannot be escaped, and we are in the realm of the Father whose heart cannot be avoided… When You are sad, we will also be sad, and when we are sad, You stand in a position of sadness. Father, when You wish to go East, we have taken a direction to go West, and we know that it is not easy for You to gather us who have taken such diverging paths.
If even humans cannot understand each other, how much sacrifice must You invest to open a way for understanding between Yourself and humanity? When we think about this, we realize that the effort required is not just dozens or hundreds of times, but thousands or even millions of times greater. When we ask who among all the people on this earth can bridge this gap and connect this place, if we find that no one can take on such responsibility, we think about how sorrowful and pitiful Heaven must be.
If there are sons and daughters who are truly determined to fulfill their duty of filial piety, they must be a group that sacrifices their lives to fill this path and to navigate it, while also striving to protect it. We come to realize that this path is the path of filial piety. Whenever we look at the diverging circumstances of the North and South and the environment that You face directly, we come to know that there is only one path we must take.
We must be prepared to protect this nation with our lives and to show the nation You desire, holding hands with Heaven and ensuring that no one falls behind. When we think about this, we realize that we must fulfill such a mission today. However, we are powerless. We are weak, but when the compassionate heart of Heaven is poured out upon us, we know that there is nothing we cannot accomplish.
In lonely places, there is a Father who wishes to comfort us with a heart of encouragement, and in sorrowful places, there is a Father who comes with a heart of mercy, and in places of deep anguish, there is a Father who shows us patience. Because of this, the path of restoration that we must endure is still open before us. If the North and South cannot bear with each other, then religious people must take responsibility. If there is no one among the religious who can take such responsibility, please gather this pitiful group and have them bear that responsibility.
This path is the final path, and it must be the last wish that You desire, right? Those who wish to take responsibility for that place are not those who seek to live or to be happy. They will have to face criticism and ridicule from both sides, and when we think about the fact that we must fulfill the responsibilities of labor for both sides, we know that we have no choice but to appeal to You with tears before You. We know that there is no other way but to hope for the manifestation of Heaven's power here.
At this time, Father, who knows our situation well, we have nothing. We have no desires that we long for. We only have a heart that wishes for the day when Your will can be fulfilled in this nation, this land, and this three-thousand-ri peninsula, so we earnestly hope and desire that You may manifest and guide us.
Father! When we think about the position of the young children who have been on this path for several years, we feel how weak and unreliable human beings are. We realize that Your position, which must rely on such humans, is thousands of times more miserable than ours.
That position can connect not only with our individual circumstances but also with history, the world, and the future. Whenever we think about the desperate situation of the Father, who must strengthen His heart every day while facing all of this emotionally, we cannot endure even a moment without feeling the pain of the Father who has come this far. If there are words that can comfort You, we must seek those words, and if there is a path of loyalty and filial piety that we must take for You, we must pursue it even if it requires research. For this reason, we must strive until the end and fight until the end. We earnestly hope and desire that You may take care of everything.
Today, since it is September 10, it can also be a day that represents the 90th. From now on, three days later, please remember Your children in North Korea who will come to this place. Even if the paths of Cain and Abel have diverged, because You have a heart that wishes to love those who come, the people in South Korea must have hearts that love them and welcome them with everything. We know that there must be a way for the laws of Heaven and the lifeline of Heaven to manifest in the hearts of each individual or to those who represent the entire population of North Korea.
12   The Path of a Filial Son
Father, if there are those who betray this path and oppose it, we earnestly hope and desire that You may be a righteous judge based on justice, distinguishing between good and evil in that position. We earnestly hope and desire that everything this nation expects and hopes for during this period may not be in vain.
If there are those who are placed on this path and cannot follow this will, Father, please stop them. We know that when You touch them with a heart of love, the content of indemnity that can be resolved will overflow, and there will be nothing You cannot accomplish. We have been those who have set out to offer our sincerity until that day, but how can anyone be able to offer a sincerity that can align with the wishes You desire?
Because we must at least pretend or imitate, Father, who remembers our pitiful selves, please do not abandon their wishes and intentions, and we earnestly hope and desire that You may remember the future path of this nation.
Father! This place is the headquarters of the Unification Church. This place is where we know that if we have caused great pain to Your heart, it is a place that has caused pain, and if we have caused sorrow, it is a place that has caused sorrow.
If Your heart is here, we know that we must be in a position where we cannot hide our disloyalty before that heart, and we must be those who know that there is a path we must fulfill before You.
This place is a fearful place. Your children scattered throughout the nation are offering their sincerity while looking towards this place, so please repay them a millionfold. We also know that Your beloved children scattered overseas are praying towards this place. When we consider that they are anxiously hoping for Korea to improve while directly facing the will and destiny of this nation, Father, please let Your love not be severed among them.
While there are those who curse us, there are also foreign people who share our bloodline praying for us. Moreover, when we think about the fact that spirits in the spiritual world are eagerly watching over us, we realize that we are not alone. We know that behind us is the strong and courageous power of Heaven's compassion, and we know that behind us are billions of spirits watching over us. Please allow us to fulfill our sincerity before their wishes and desires, and let us fulfill our duty of filial piety before You.
Father! At this time, we confess everything before You and humbly bow down, longing for Your gracious gifts. Without the shock of Heaven's deep heart rising up within us, we cannot recover or advance. We earnestly hope and desire that You may increase Heaven's power and manifest the ties of life.
This morning, knowing that You love this nation and this people, we earnestly hope and desire that You may grant blessings upon those who pray. May Your children who are bowing down here become one heart and one mind, preparing for the destined path that will come in the future, and may they humbly receive Your whip if there is a whip, or receive praise if there is praise, and may they fulfill their duty of filial piety as sons and daughters.
May the year 1972 become a blessing in the future. Father, we think about the fact that the second seven-year course has only a few months left. Considering that this period is an age where global issues are diverging and losing direction, we earnestly hope and desire that we may be heavenly sons and daughters who can firmly stand in one place and steadily take a united direction towards the purpose for which You desire.
We ask that You oversee everything and transfer the will You have permitted into our hearts, and we pray in the name of True Parents. Amen.
<Words> The Path of a Filial Son… Please do not feel disappointed that the filial daughter is missing.
the one who takes on the most important responsibilities among them is the true filial child. 

The path of a filial child is not just about receiving love from parents, but also about fulfilling the hopes and dreams that parents have for their children. A true filial child understands the sacrifices made by their parents and strives to repay that love through their actions and responsibilities.

In this way, the relationship between parents and children is a reflection of the greater relationship between humanity and God. Just as parents desire the best for their children, God desires the best for humanity. This divine relationship is rooted in love, and it is through understanding and embodying this love that we can grow closer to God.

The teachings of filial piety emphasize the importance of respect, gratitude, and responsibility towards one's parents. These values are essential not only for personal growth but also for the well-being of society as a whole. When children honor their parents, they contribute to a harmonious family environment, which in turn fosters a peaceful community.

As we reflect on the significance of being a filial child, we must also recognize the broader implications of our actions. By embodying the principles of filial piety, we not only honor our parents but also fulfill our role as responsible members of society. This creates a cycle of love and respect that extends beyond the family unit and into the world.

In conclusion, the path of a filial child is a journey of love, responsibility, and growth. It is a commitment to honoring our parents while also striving to fulfill our potential as individuals and as members of the larger human family. By embracing this path, we can contribute to a better world for ourselves and future generations.
Who is the best filial child? Among the ten duties of parents, if one takes on the most difficult task and says, "I will take responsibility for this. I will solve this problem and love my parents," then that son can be remembered by his parents more than any other son. The more such a son exists, the closer he gets to the position of being a filial child.

When viewed this way, a person who wants to fulfill the duty of filial piety by doing easy tasks in an easy position is not as commendable as a responsible person who wants to take on the difficult tasks of filial piety. The one who stands in such a position, such sons and daughters, are the ones who have entered the path of filial piety. This is undeniable.

God is currently watching the world closely. What is the most pressing issue for God? Of course, minor personal issues are problems, but what is the bigger issue? It is global events. It is a global problem. From God's perspective, who has the responsibility to save humanity, the current situation of South Korea may be important to the people of South Korea, but if there is something that can solve a bigger global problem, God will devote all His efforts and attention to that.

When viewed this way, since God is concerned about global issues, if someone is willing to take responsibility for global problems, then that person is standing closer to God than any nation or individual. This is beyond question. Therefore, the position of a filial child is a position that represents the responsibility for the suffering of parents.

If there is something good, the good should be excluded, and the path of a filial child is to always take responsibility for the bad. The path of a loyal subject is the same. When there is a ruler, and that ruler is faced with the most troubling issues, the duty of loyalty begins when someone steps forward to take responsibility for those issues. A sage transcends the nation and stands in a position that is beyond any single ethnicity or nation, and if there is a path that can be a concern before God, it is not someone who wants to avoid the most miserable position but someone who wants to take responsibility for that miserable position. If such a person exists, then they can become the greatest among sages. This is an undeniable fact.

The current time and the position of contemporary religion
Today, there are democratic and communist worlds. The democratic world is already struggling to find its way, and the communist world is also in a conflicting position. 

If there is a God who looks upon these two worlds, where will God place His heart? Until now, religion has come forth for God, and religious people have struggled to walk the path of filial piety for God. However, now, when we look at numerous religions, we see that religion has already entered the autumn season. We are witnessing the phenomenon of leaves turning colors and falling.

God cannot help but think of those who are on His side rather than those who are on their own side. We know that the communist world stands on a materialistic perspective that denies the existence of God. Among the two worlds, God would place hope in those who believe that there is a God. However, the democratic world is agreeing with the materialistic perspective that denies the existence of God.

Currently, society acknowledges that religion has become corrupt. Even among conscientious people in society, they can claim, "I am better than any religious person." In such a position, can God have any expectation that they will fulfill the duty of filial piety? There can be no expectation. Why? Because if there is a heaven, there is no religion that steps forward to take responsibility for the concerns of the heavenly parent. Those who do not do this cannot inherit the path of filial piety. Therefore, we must recognize that this is the time when we must surpass the position of the early church.

Jesus prayed profoundly, saying, "Abba Father! If it is possible, let this cup pass from me. Yet not my will, but yours be done." We know that even in that moment of intense prayer before life and death, He could not resolve the issue of a nation.

We know that the Israelites opposed Him, and despite His struggles, He could not avoid the fate that led Him to the cross. We understand that even in the face of a nation's destiny, Jesus could not resolve it through His final prayer.

However, what time is it now? It is not a national time but a global time. In this global time, the sense of mission cannot be felt centered around a nation. It is not a position that pursues the mission of religion from the standpoint of being responsible for a nation. The time now is to transcend national perspectives and focus on a global perspective, to be a son who can pray, "Abba Father! If it is possible, not according to our nation's will—it's not my will—but according to your will."

Now is the time to pray for God's will beyond nations and the world. Look at Jesus. He was betrayed by His nation, betrayed by the church, surrounded by His people, and left alone. The position of being left alone is not a place where one can say, "This is our will."

He took three disciples with Him, but Jesus did not pray in the same position as them. Why? If He had become a supporter and companion in spirit, He should have prayed together with them, yet the very act of praying separately revealed that they were not united.

If He had prayed, "Let us not do according to our will, but according to the Father's will," in the same position as the three disciples, Jesus would not have been a pitiful figure. Isn't that so? After three years of public life, His final prayer was, "Let this cup pass from me, yet not my will, but yours be done." Jesus' will must not remain only as His own will. It must become our will, the will of the nation, and the will of the world. Because He was left alone, He could not help but speak of His own will. That position of Jesus was indeed miserable.

We must think about how heaven felt toward such a son, such a Jesus. The issue now is not about Jesus facing the nation of Israel or Judaism. When viewed globally, isn't the nation of Israel similar to today's democratic world? Isn't Christianity similar to Judaism? Isn't communism similar to Rome? Communism is attacking Christianity from within and without, binding it with chains. The environment has developed globally in a way that resembles the relationships surrounding Jesus 2,000 years ago.

Now, facing such an end-of-century situation... this is a major issue that God must resolve. It is a global event that God must take responsibility for. Then, how serious must God's position be when looking at these issues? In such a situation, can one say, "Abba Father... let this cup pass from me, yet not my will, but yours be done"? Can one pray, "Bend your will to our nation's will"?

Now is the time to transcend the individual, the family, the nation, and the world. If we are to pray now, what kind of prayer should we offer? Of course, we must pray for the world, but we must also pray to liberate the spirits in the spiritual realm. There must be people who pray such prayers.

One should not pray, "Abba Father! Please act according to the will of our Unification Church." Our will must become the will of the world. Our will must become the will of Heaven. In a position that unites both inside and outside, with a sense of responsibility, can there be a believer who can say, "Let us not do according to my will"? If such a person does not exist, then Jesus' will has failed. Because Jesus could not expand His will from His own will to the will of the family, the nation, and the world, He returned in failure.

Is there a denomination or sect today that can take responsibility for the world?
Even if there are many Christians around the world, how many can pray, "Let this cup pass from me, yet not my will, but yours be done"? Is there anyone who can say, "Let us do according to our nation's will and according to Heaven's will"? It would not be an exaggeration to conclude that there is no one.

In such a time, if there are people in our Unification Church who pray with that standard and are willing to give their lives to fulfill that will, what will God do? Will He welcome them or not? If God exists, He cannot help but welcome such people.

Therefore, the path of our Unification Church is not a path for oneself. It is not a path for one's family. It is not a path for one's nation alone. It is a path for the world. If the world lives, the nation lives. If the nation lives, the ethnicity lives. If the ethnicity lives, the family lives. If the family lives, the individual lives. Only when the world lives can everything else live.

Then, is there a denomination on this earth that can be praised before the world? From God's perspective, is there a denomination that can be recognized as, "My beloved ones! You alone can take responsibility for the world"? There is no such denomination.

Today in Korea, we know there are numerous sects. Even if we examine all those sects, both the leading pastors and the congregants are unable to transcend the boundaries of their own children. They cannot go beyond the walls of their own churches. They are unable to surpass that.

While one person may fight for their life, fearing that someone might take their congregants, there is no pastor who cries out to unite the religions and break down the barriers of individuals for the sake of the nation. Such a flock does not exist. Chasing after the walls of one's own church is akin to falling into a trap, and this is the current state of affairs.

If this continues, it will lead to destruction, so if there is a heaven, there must be some action taken. The church must be liberated. To liberate the church, faith must be liberated. If the foundation of faith is wrong, it must be struck down. Only by breaking this down and scattering it can there be a chance for re-education; otherwise, there is no way to save it. This is an unavoidable situation. Those who say, "My church! My church! My denomination! My denomination!" must be struck down.

Look, Jacob had twelve brothers, and they fought among themselves, didn't they? Would their parents have been happy to see that? Today, the same situation exists with Catholicism, Presbyterianism, Methodism... they are enemies. Our Unification Church transcends the concept of denominations. We are not fighting for the sake of denominations. Our purpose is different.

God seeks to find the nation He desires, even if He loses the church. Even if He loses the nation, He seeks to find the world He desires. The path is clearly set. There will be no one who can claim they do not know this path. So, who can stand close to God? It is those who fight for the world. It is those who take responsibility for the world.

North and South must unify with a national perspective that encompasses the world.
In this time of division between North and South... you all know that representatives from North Korea will be coming soon. Can the two Koreas, standing in such different positions, become one? Is there anyone with true patriotism who loves the Korea that true Koreans desire? Whether it is centered around South Korea or North Korea... there is absolutely no way to unify while defending one's own position. That is something that should not be attempted from the start. Even if attempted, it would be difficult. When such a method fails, both sides become weaker. The more they go back and forth, the weaker they become.

Even if the Korean issue is resolved, it cannot be solved solely as a Korean issue. It is connected to global issues. The global problem must be resolved first. No matter how much North and South exchange and establish a form of unification, it cannot become an ideal nation.

They must receive recommendations from various countries around the world. To do this, the people of South Korea must have a national perspective that can encompass and assimilate the people of North Korea. They cannot remain with a national perspective that only stays within the boundaries of the Republic of Korea. If there is a national perspective that can encompass the world, then the unification of the Republic of Korea can align with the unification of the world. This is how it will be.

From this perspective, the positions held by North and South cannot be maintained. This applies to nations, denominations, and churches alike. 

If there is a God who faces such realities, what would be the means by which He hopes to resolve them? In other words, what command can God give to a filial child who can take responsibility for such issues? That is the question.

To solve this difficult problem, if it requires sacrificing one's life, then it must be the heart of the parents that desires such sacrifice. Isn't that so?

The vertical will of God is to save the horizontal world.
Parents always want to keep their beloved children close. If one continues in a one-to-one relationship with a father-son dynamic, the nation will disappear, and the world will disappear; thus, the child cannot help but be placed in a position of sacrifice. The reason Jesus died on the cross was for such a purpose. Ultimately, He was placed in the position of death because of God's will. What is that will? It is not to save the nation of Israel but to save the world.

How is the father-son relationship established? It is not only between parents and children. That relationship is only a vertical relationship. The horizontal relationship cannot be established. The horizontal issues must include individuals, families, ethnicities, nations, and the world. Only after resolving the horizontal issues can the vertical issues be resolved. It is not that the vertical issues are resolved first and then the horizontal issues; rather, the horizontal issues must be resolved first for the vertical issues to be resolved.

When viewed through Jesus, Israel and Judaism must unite to establish a horizontal foundation...
to the world. The person who can take responsibility for the most difficult issues in front of their parents is considered a filial child. Just as mentioned earlier, when the most challenging problem arises in front of parents, there are those who struggle to take responsibility for it, and that person is called a filial child. Being a filial child is not limited to a specific individual; anyone can become one.

Today, there are Christian denominations that boast of traditional histories, such as Catholicism, Methodism, and Presbyterianism. Just because someone is a certain person's child does not make them a filial child. A filial child can be anyone.

What kind of person is a filial child? It is someone who can take responsibility for new and significant tasks from a higher position, someone who is willing to act in situations that require responsibility for new and difficult matters. The path to becoming a filial child is always open. No matter how young one may be, or how newly established a church may be, if they can do what others cannot, they become a filial child. If one can take on all the responsibilities that others cannot, God will surely use that person. That person will be called a filial child.

In that sense, the established churches and the Unification Church are different. From that perspective, you should feel a sense of pride. (There is a brief moment of silence in the recording.) When we go from the South to the North and say, "Let's do as we wish," they do not want to do it. They also do not want unification when it means they will incur losses. They seek what can be mutually beneficial. Isn't that right? We need to find what can benefit each other. In the context of human society and the history of our nation, there is no way to find that.

That is why the signboard of the Unification Church is not the issue. The signboard can be removed at any time. Even if the title of the Republic of Korea disappears, if it becomes a nation that can dominate the world, it could be given a name higher than the Republic of Korea. Isn't that so? Who would refuse that? Who would dislike exchanging it for something greater and better?

From this standpoint, our Unification Church must move forward. We must walk the path of a filial child. Then, centered on the world issues that God is concerned about, we must consider how we can experience and take on the responsibility of those world issues from Heaven's perspective.

To be a filial child, one must always align with the heart of the parents. To walk the path of a filial child means not to act in a way that is disconnected from the parents. If the parents go east, one must go east; if the parents go west, one must go west. If, while going, the purpose is presented and then suddenly told to turn back, one must turn back. There should be no objections to that. Even if one is told to turn back ten times, they must turn back and follow.

"Ah! What kind of parents are these? They turn back ten times and change their minds ten times. Oh! Father and Mother, this doesn't sit well with me." If one rebels like that, they cannot fulfill their duty as a filial child. If the parents are acting foolishly, the children must also act foolishly. If it is a command from the parents, even if it seems foolish, it must be done. The act of foolishness itself is not acceptable, but if the parents are unaware, it is one thing, but if they know and still act, that is another matter.

Then why do parents act foolishly? Because to select the best among the filial children, that is the only way. If there are a hundred filial children, the parents will act foolishly to create the best among them. They will turn back a hundred times and change their minds a hundred times. They may even change their minds a thousand times. However, if one recognizes that those changes are real and dedicates their life to absolutely obeying the commands of those parents, they can become the king of filial children. They can become the ruler among filial children. Wouldn't that be the case?

When that happens, one must be able to recognize such foolishness as their calling. "Ah! This doesn't fit my reasoning, so I don't understand." If one thinks like that, the path of a filial child will be blocked. The path of a filial child will be cut off. Therefore, there must be a global path of filial piety that can overcome the highest obstacles. That is what it will be.

We are a group that seeks and strives to find the path of the best filial child. Then what kind of being is God? God is the parent of humanity, and God is the king of kings among humanity, and God is the center of all things. To become a child of that God... If we look at it from the perspective of an individual, centered on a family, one is a filial child, but that filial child must become a global filial child. Isn't that so?

If there are loyal subjects, God must be the one who leads the representative loyal subjects on a global scale. God must also lead the representatives of the sages on a global scale. When this happens, God becomes the highest.

This does not happen separately; that one being can be both a parent and a king and everything else. Isn't God the central being that encompasses all three requirements?

Then, if only those who can represent the highest filial piety, the highest loyalty, and the highest holiness can serve God, it cannot be done separately. God's desire is for a person who fulfills all three at once. A person who can be a filial child, a loyal subject, and the greatest of saints.

So how can such a person be selected? Personally, they must be brought to the point of death. They must be someone who can act in a way that is right, regardless of who commands or opposes them.

From this perspective, there is no doubt that God is such a being. We are striving to fulfill our roles as children of that God. Our Path of Restoration
It has been nearly two years since the 777 families received the blessing.

Members are people bound by one situation and one heart. You are undoubtedly members of the Unification Church. To be a member means that you must live in one house and be bound by one situation and one heart.

In other words, if one of the brothers falls ill, the other brothers must be concerned about the sick brother, and even if they are in an isolated position, they must share in the situation of the sick brother. Parents cannot be indifferent to the situation of a sick child either. They cannot avoid participating in that situation. Therefore, if you are a member, you cannot stand apart from any situation, whether it is difficult or joyful.

If there is sad news for the parents, that sadness inevitably becomes the sadness of the children. Even if someone says that the parents have nothing to do with them, such a statement does not hold.

If parents are sad and worried, even if the children are scattered everywhere and have different duties, they will inevitably share in the parents' worries from their own positions. The more heartfelt the filial heart of the child towards the parents, the more they cannot spend a day without being affected by the parents' suffering, even if they work in different places. If there is a child among them who worries more deeply and more about the parents, that child is closer to the parents.

Therefore, the child who deeply understands the parents' sadness will earnestly hope for the alleviation of that sadness and wish for the resolution of that concern beyond the environment they are in. Even if they have their own sadness, if they have a heart that wishes for the parents' sadness to be resolved before their own, that person can be called a filial child. However, if both the parents and the child have concerns, and the child thinks, "The parents should consider my concerns," prioritizing their own concerns over the parents', that person is not one with the parents.

From the perspective of the principle of filial piety, a person who forgets the position of the parents cannot form a significant bond with them. If a child demands that their own sadness be acknowledged while disregarding the parents' sadness, they cannot be a filial child and become an unfilial child. This is something we often experience in our daily lives or family life.

So, what is a true brother? A true brother is someone who feels the difficulties of their sibling more deeply than their own difficulties when their sibling is in a difficult situation.
What is the value of being a filial child? While one may have their own difficulties, they should be more concerned about their parents' hardships, not treating their own difficulties as a problem. Even if they stand in a position where they add their parents' worries on top of their own, if they can digest and accept this as a natural occurrence, isn't that where the path of filial piety begins? When a child neglects their parents' difficulties and distances themselves, that is where a rupture occurs. This is the emergence of the path of unfilial conduct, not the path of filial piety. When siblings do not prioritize their brothers' difficulties over their own, the relationship between siblings becomes estranged. This is how it is viewed.

In this perspective of restoration providence or restoration history, what kind of person is God seeking? God is undoubtedly looking for a filial child. And what kind of person have we humans truly been seeking until now? When looking among friends for someone we can respect, what kind of person is that? When I have worries, it is someone who can worry about my worries even more than I do. If I am in a position of sacrifice and hardship, if I have an older brother or younger sibling who can take responsibility for that position, there is no one better than that sibling.

If we were to summarize human life, humans are like siblings, and heaven is in the position of parents. So, what kind of person is needed among siblings? It is someone who does not put their own worries first but is willing to take on their siblings' worries as well. Isn't that the kind of person many people are looking for in this world? Everything culminates in that one statement. Everything comes down to that one statement...

Then, what kind of person is a good friend? It is someone who can always take on my difficulties for me. It is someone who can always look after my convenience. When I am in difficulty, if that friend also says they are having a hard time, and stands in the position of "I am having a hard time too, so why worry?" then they cannot appear as a friend who can be there in difficult times. A true friend who can be called a good friend is someone who, even while in a difficult position, forgets their own difficulties and stands in a position to take on their friend's difficulties. We cannot deny that this is the only way to determine a good friend and a good person. This is all we need to do.

Restoration history has been managed through the parent-child relationship centered on parents. If we look at restoration history or anything else, in a straightforward manner... what kind of existence is Abel, and what kind of existence is Cain? If we talk about Cain and Abel in our principles, Cain is someone who, when they have worries, tries to impose those worries on others, while Abel is someone who, although they have their own worries, is willing to take on the worries of others. That is the difference, that difference.

Then, what has God been doing with religion, culture, or morality until now? What is the purpose? What kind of person is He trying to create? He is trying to create someone like Abel. 

If one becomes a person who says they will take responsibility for their own difficulties and, while overcoming their own difficulties, also takes on the difficulties of others, then they can become siblings that their parents can be happy about. If that family is a peaceful and happy family, then no matter how many children there are before one parent, if those children are willing to take responsibility for each other's difficulties without passing their own difficulties onto their siblings and are willing to inherit their siblings' difficulties, then that family can be called a happy family. Moreover, if siblings can say they will take responsibility for each other, at the same time, when it comes to their parents, if they can set aside their own difficulties and come together as siblings to say, "Even if we have our own difficulties, we will take on our parents' difficulties," then that is the play of restoration history.

If two siblings can come together and say, "Let us take on our parents' difficulties," then they can welcome their parents. What is the history of Cain and Abel? When the two become one, they can welcome their parents. Then what will they do when they become one? Because they have traditionally trained to care for each other, they can serve each other, and when there are difficulties for their parents, they can stand in a position to say, "We will take responsibility for our difficulties and also for our parents' difficulties." Only then can they truly become one. Only then can the way to welcome their parents emerge. This is it. The essence is nothing more than this.

Ultimately, if we reduce it, we can conclude that history has been managed through the parent-child relationship centered on parents, within a family relationship. When we look at the world from this principle, the world is merely a broader application of this formal principle.

Because they have received blessings, they can enter the rebirth gate of heaven, but they cannot leave from there. It is fortunate that they do not know... They do not even realize how fortunate they are, and later, even if they cry out, "Save me," no one will save them. Because of such things, the teacher has suffered throughout his life, and Jesus gave his life for this. "Those who seek to lose their life will find it..." This is the miserable position where one must make a final decision, and that is why they were prepared to face even the path of death. It is a serious path. You are not here to play around, thinking it is fine either way, like time flowing by. If you play around, there is only death. Such people will inevitably be buried upside down in their graves.

I have told you everything, so you cannot say, "Why didn't the teacher tell me it would be like this?" Do you understand? You will not be able to speak, whether dead or alive. However, I have a responsibility to speak, which is why I have come here today. In fact, I did not want to come here. I woke up early and found that time had already passed. Still, because I have taken responsibility, I felt I had to come and at least say something. I started speaking now to urge you to understand what kind of work is being done, what position we are in, and what resolutions need to be made, even if it is unpleasant, so that you can make a resolution to run. Do you understand? "Yes." If you cannot do that, you will become foolish people who do not exist in this world. 

We must align with the providential time.
Right now, you can go as you please, but at that time, you will not even be able to crawl. Right now, you can walk and move freely, but at that time, you will not be able to come and go. There will come a time when you will not even be able to crawl well. Those who have not fulfilled their responsibilities will be removed from the list of the 777 couples' joint marriage ceremony, and all photos will be destroyed. If there are such people, it will bring dirt upon us.

If you make a mistake and go out into society to have a worldly marriage and have children, do you think heaven will look upon that favorably? They will treat you as Satan. You do not know the heavenly laws that will unfold in your future, and this is a shocking path, right here. If it is frightening, there is nothing more frightening than this. This is the final path. The teacher knows this content, which is why he has tried to walk the path of God absolutely, even in places where he has bled and suffered all kinds of torture. He held onto that and was willing to die for it; he was not someone who would die while letting it go. Once you let go, it is hard to grab it again. Adam lost the path once, and it took thousands of years of effort to regain it, didn’t it? Therefore, if you let go even once, it will be a big problem. Humans are foolish. They do not know when their destiny will be decided. Isn’t that right? "Yes." Do you live knowing when the sun rises every day, or do you not? How many times have you thought, "Ah! The sun is rising now"? The last equinox was on the 23rd, and that was the day when the lengths of day and night were equal, but that moment when day and night are equal is shorter than the tick of a clock. Isn’t that right? If it exists, it seems like it does, and if it does not exist, it seems like it does not. No one knows that moment for real. And you do not even realize that you are getting sick and that your health is declining. Do you know? You do not. No matter how capable you think you are, you do not know when the time of judgment for your destiny, the origin of your life’s rise and fall, and its peak will come. A wise person is someone who prepares to align with that. Such a person can live when others die.

In that respect, the teacher is someone who lives more sensitively than anyone else regarding time. At what point will a certain time come, and to capture that, he works harder than anyone else. That is why, to not miss the time, he has been developing work until now in accordance with the time.

Have you ever had a moment where your life was at stake? Have you ever experienced a time when your life was on the line, where you were unsure whether you would live or die, and where heaven and earth were in turmoil? Have you ever spent a night without sleep, feeling that tension? Have you? No, right? That is why you have passed through safely. You think everything has already been settled. The teacher, who bears such responsibilities today, does he think he can just sleep like you and do whatever? Not a chance. He must align with the time.

In the history of indemnity restoration, to indemnify, offerings must be made, right? To make offerings, there must be an Adam representative, conditional objects, and a period is absolutely necessary. You are Adam representatives. Therefore, conditional objects are needed, and what kind of conditional objects? Material conditional objects and human conditional objects. Isn’t that right? Conditional objects are offerings, aren’t they? That is the three great sons and daughters. They must be completely separated from the world of Satan and established on your side. But it cannot be done carelessly at any time. If it is seven years, it must be seven years; if it is 40 days, it must be 40 days. There is a definite period. Is there a period or not? There is.

The path of destiny that must reach the world during the third seven-year course.
That is why, during the period of the third seven-year course, we must walk the path of destiny that must reach the world. The teacher is saying, "Time, do not go." It is not "Go." It is "Do not go." Even if a day feels like a thousand years, before the 21 years are up, we must establish the conditions for indemnity restoration that will change the global landscape. I understand this as my lifelong mission, to what extent the Unification Church can influence ten nations. Do you think it is easy to connect the world in 21 years when it is hard to connect even one nation? It requires hard work to lay that foundation. Do you think you can just transfer it to God without any effort? Not a chance. You must have a conditional foundation as solid as a cornerstone. That is why conditional objects are needed, and a period is absolutely necessary. Isn’t that right?
The teacher says that if you just pass the age of 40, it will be a big problem. So, in a hurry... If you accidentally pass it, everything will just drop off. You probably don’t know how serious it was. Until the first 7-year course period was established as God's day, you wouldn’t know how serious it was. That’s all the path you have to take.

The second 7-year course is about the nation... Because Jesus could not stand in a position to save the country centered on the nation and people, the responsibility to restore this lies with you, the members of the Unification Church. The teacher doesn’t have to do it. It’s your responsibility. If you fail to take responsibility, you will fall into ruin like the nation of Israel. During the third 7-year course period, if the democratic world does not create a position where it can raise the flag within the heavenly realm, there will be a game where heads will roll in front of the world’s communists. That’s how it is. Israel could not take responsibility and wandered for 2,000 years, right? Did they or didn’t they? “They did.” If you cannot take responsibility during the second 7-year course, would that be good for you? Would that be good or bad? “Bad.” If it were good, the principle would be a lie. If it were good, I wouldn’t have to suffer. That’s why we need to make a decision during these three years.

From now on, during the three-year period, blessed families must fulfill their responsibilities. Are we not negotiating between the North and South now? Can you trust this country, this nation? You cannot trust it. The urgent situation is right in front of our eyes. We are entering a time when we can show whether the words of the principle are true or not. Would God bless those who cannot take responsibility even while seeing this in front of their eyes? No way. Knowing that, I must fulfill my responsibilities. You can choose to know or not know, to sleep or rest, do as you please. The teacher has a busy path to walk. Even if you do not match the pace with the teacher, there are countries that can match the pace. Jesus’ time was a national era, but the teacher’s time is a global era. Do you understand? “Yes.” There are plenty of countries that can match the pace, so it won’t perish.

If we center around the mobilization team and act for just three years, we can have a significant impact on the world and create major issues in one country. Once we enter that position, we believe that any country can welcome us. In this urgent providential and decisive end time, what will you look forward to? At this time, what you think is good can become an enemy. The Bible says that your household members are enemies, and that refers to the members of the Unification Church. Women must fulfill their responsibilities as women of restoration, which is why nursing mothers will be harmed. They cannot go the right way...

That’s why when two people are together, one will be taken and one will be left behind. One person next to you can go, but another cannot. If the husband cannot take responsibility between the husband and wife, the wife must abandon that husband to go the path of the will to survive. Such games will unfold. Everything must be fulfilled according to the Bible. Isn’t that so?

That’s why the biblical saying “Those who seek to lose their life will find it, and those who seek to save their life will lose it” must be fulfilled. Who must fulfill it? The Unification Church must fulfill it. The teacher has done such work until now.

So, you must walk the path the teacher has walked. The teacher’s path is long and takes time, but you must establish even a short condition of indemnity in the same way, right? That’s unavoidable. The 777 couples you received are the 3rd blessing, the 33rd family, the 72nd family, the 120th family, the 430th family, and then about 43 families during the world tour, culminating in the 777 families. So, domestically, it is the 7th blessing ceremony, and globally, it is the 8th blessing ceremony. This blessing ceremony is also the last one. Therefore, it is 777 families. And what date is it? “The 21st.” That’s also three times seven is twenty-one (3×7=21). This is the last hurdle. I can now not bless you. That’s why I involved ten countries. Isn’t that so?

From that perspective, focusing on the connection of blessings, if they live according to the will like Jesus who resurrected with authority, the nation centered on the ten nations will remain. If you are faithful to the will, God will surely bless you. Jesus could not bind the ten tribes, right? He could not marry the twelve representatives of the ten tribes, right? But the teacher has bound the ten nations. The number ten corresponds to the number twelve. Isn’t that so?

Now the Unification Church will not perish. That’s why the world is entering the fortune of the Unification Church. Because of the games played in the 70s, centered on the 3-year course, to globalize the family fortune centered on Adam and Eve, we have deployed 1,200 families nationwide. This is the beginning of such a game to align with the heavenly providence. If you support well, that will connect to families. To lay the foundation for the nation, if you elevate the wife, it will connect to the family and children. That is a period that can forgive all wrongdoings and set a period of indemnity.

However, if the wives cannot witness to twelve people, they must replace their husbands to witness to twelve people. Do you understand what I mean? If not, the wives cannot return. If you want the wives to return, the husbands must fulfill their responsibilities. Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.” However, when the men go out, the teacher does not cooperate at all. The women receive cooperation because the teacher has taken responsibility. Do you understand? Helping those who went out to witness from the Unification Church is something that has never happened in history. Do you know that? Did they help before? They did not help. But this time, the teacher must help. I cannot help much, but I must help a little. So, you must help more than the teacher and the headquarters. The 2,000 won you help is three times seven is twenty-one (3×7=21), a numerical value. If you exceed the number twenty-eight, it will be okay. That’s why the headquarters started with 800 won. Otherwise, it will not connect.

Because of women, Adam fell, and the archangel fell, right? It is about restoring that. It is about being able to rise one level through women... Receiving God’s cooperation, the archangel will expand the foundation of the people centered on God’s grace. It is all principled. It is not just haphazard. Do you think such a skilled Satan will just retreat?

Now the time has come. This time, when the female members are active, they must witness to twelve people and unite before the church leader and the will. After saying that the church leader must stand in the position of the archangel, I sent them out. Isn’t that so? If they do not unite and fight, they cannot witness. If that happens, everyone will get sick and retreat.

As you all know, during this three-year period, many people in public office, God’s special people, will sacrifice. Many people went to the spiritual world this time due to unexpected accidents, right? That is all to forgive what you could not take responsibility for, and God is taking them as offerings. Those who do not know that sacrificing offerings while sitting still must face wrath. Look. Has there ever been a year with so many people dying from misfortunes like this year? “Yes.” Do you know why? They will enter heaven. The teacher has known in advance how many will be sacrificed. The principle of indemnity and restoration does not allow for forgiveness.

There is no forgiveness in the principle of indemnity and restoration.

Then why do Unification Church members have to go through such things? You must know that now is your time in the Unification Church. During the teacher’s family’s 7-year course, the teacher’s family suffered, but now we have entered your family’s time. Such and such a history of indemnity is because the principle is like that. The official cannot just pass by, so when you fail to fulfill your responsibilities, to whom will you leave the consequences? If you go somewhere for no reason and give someone a plow-like object, and it goes wrong and causes a murder or robbery, you become an accomplice. Isn’t that so? You never thought about it, but if that happens, you become an accomplice. Is that so or not? Similarly, joining the Unification Church is good, but when it leads to bad results, you must know that it affects your ancestors up to the 70th generation. It affects all your sons and daughters. You must clearly understand that such a tremendous connection inside and out is flipping over you, who is insignificant. Do you understand? This is not a threat. Just wait and see if the teacher’s words are right or wrong.

So, from this standpoint, will you fulfill your responsibilities or not? “I will.” Just like the saying “Those who seek to lose their life will find it, and those who seek to save their life will lose it,” the time has come to be prepared to risk your life. From this standpoint, through this conference, we must prepare a new resolution and new attitude, criticize the past, and face the current heavenly fortune. Thus, knowing that it is a solemn time when I must critically evaluate my position for tomorrow and judge my fate myself, I have spoken these words with the hope of establishing a solution. Do you understand? Today, I spoke about the background of what the teacher is doing.

<Prayer> Beloved Father, when we think about how you have worked hard to prepare tomorrow’s defense line while tracing our path in the midst of countless paths of suffering that no one knows, we are always humbled and sorry before you. When we think that your will, to prepare a new origin of 2,000 years of history, comes to us who did not know its value, please forgive us.

Now the position where the Unification Church can stand is firmly being established on the world stage. The authority we must show and the path we must take have already been clearly determined, so we must realize that whether we go or not depends not on anyone else but on ourselves, and there is a 5% path of restoration that we must take responsibility for. Moreover, when we look at the flat world, we must clearly realize that the connections of individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world are weighing on us today centered on us. Of course, families are precious, and knowledge is precious, but the heart that worries about the will centered on the nation, the world, the cosmos, and the Father must always take precedence to be bound to a good and more valuable position, and we have learned this in various ways. May this opportunity to learn such content be a blessing to us, and may it allow us to become better sons and daughters before the Father.

Now, let each of us realize that we cannot avoid being losers if we do not run toward the final racetrack within the designated time, and let us be aware of this undeniable fact that remains with us at this moment. Above all, we must worry about tomorrow’s numbers, tomorrow’s shame, and tomorrow’s ruin. While looking forward to the day of victory with the Father’s help, even if it becomes a painful life, let us resolve to overcome it and become your sons who can fight with gratitude.

Through this gathering, may you allow this nation and this people to be a source of joy for you, and may those who are currently out in the field witnessing be provided with a new origin that can be a source of strength and pride.

When the work we do through the second 7-year course is extended, we know well that it can only bring sad results before the Father. From a principled standpoint, we know that to offer a sacrifice, a central figure is needed, conditions are needed, and a period is needed, so please do not forget that we have a heavy and serious responsibility to adapt before this nation, this people, and this world through the second 7-year course. We earnestly hope and desire that we may devote ourselves day and night for that purpose. Even if I forget the time I eat and the time I sleep, I must not forget this, which is the ideology and mental attitude of the sons and daughters standing in the position of following the Unification thought, which I did not realize until now. Please allow me to know this from now on.

When we think about the glorious nation that our descendants desire for the liberation of this country tomorrow, we must realize that we are standing in a solemn position where we must affirm that fate. We must clench our fists with all our might and rise up. Let them newly realize that there are national responsibilities and historical responsibilities in the world. Thus, may we become sons and daughters who can stand proudly with the appearance of the Father’s soldiers for tomorrow’s victors.

There may have been sad events in the past, but we know well that we cannot avoid colliding with eternal sadness in the future if we escape from the current sadness. Now, we declare our determination and resolution to go justly for all the goals of tomorrow, so please guide us according to your will.

Not only may we be welcomed as victorious sons and daughters in a place of impossible results, but may we also be blessed to be praised as sons and daughters who cannot help but receive love by offering victorious results before you. We earnestly request and desire your guidance and education.

May you joyfully accept everything today, and may these individuals be able to show their joyful selves before the Father through their own self-awareness felt in the words. I humbly offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen. *
